bdce say:

I have a Lumia 950 (AT&T version).  Sometimes I notice that the pictures I take with the default camera result in a lower than expected resolution of 2560 x 1440.

When this happens my camera sometimes locks up, but usually it doesn't and the only way I can tell that something is wrong is when I go to preview the photo.  If I preview it right after taking the photo it is stuck on the "applying finishing touches".  If I preview later in the photos app it will have the magic wand telling me I can adjust the image, but touching the icon results in no action.

When I look at the image details the resolution is 2560 x 1440 and it doesn't have any EXIF or location information.  I think the resolution of the screen is the same so I'm wondering if maybe the camera failed to take the full picture and somehow just saves a screenshot or something.

This seems to happen regardless of whether I have live images on/off, rich capture on/off.  My setting is set to 16MP.  I have not tried setting it to 8MP and don't really want 8MP output.

I know Windows 10 has a lot of bugs.  I have a lot of other bugs, but this camera issue is pretty important to me because I bought the phone based mainly on the camera.

Mainly I just want to find out if this is a known issue.  Are other people having this issue?  If it's known and something that might get fixed later then I have no problem waiting.  But, if this is not a known issue and no one has encountered this maybe I should look at returning and exchanging the device.

The file contains 95% English letters and 5% Arabic letters.  The English letters are error free but the Arabic letters have a weird formatting which makes it impossible to read. But when I mark the word and delete the formatting the text is perfectly readable. So I need to select all Arabic letters and replace them with the same letters but without formatting. 

I know that I have to choose the Language from the advanced search and replace function -> format -> language. I tested it and MS office word finds all the Arabic letters. 

The problem is that I have no idea what I should write in the "replace with" box.  I searched the internet for a book or homepage where all the commands of search and replace functions are listed but only find pages where people ask how to use the basic find and replace function.

charleskenyon (ia) say:
Use a copy of your document.
Ctrl+H
Find - Format Language
Replace ^&

Do NOT check wildcards.

jim lty say:

Hi Raymond,

Here are some suggestions regarding the issue:
1. From the log, please confirm if the issue only happen to one specific .pptx file with OS X 10.10.5 Yosemite & Office 15.16.151105.
You may also try if the issue happen to other Macs with the same .pptx file.

2. Try creating a new user profile in your Mac to see if the issue can be resolved:
On the Apple menu, click System Preferences.
If some settings are unavailable, click the lock icon, and then type an administrator name and password.
Click Add (+), and then type the user's name.
Type a short name if you do not want to use the short name that is automatically generated.
Type the user's password in the Password and Verify boxes.
Click Limitations, and then give that user permission to administer the computer.
Log off from the current account.
Log on to the new user account.
Start the Office for Mac program, and then try to reproduce the issue again to see if it can be resolved.

3. Perform a Safe Boot and temporarily turn off other programs to make sure there's no third party/antivirus program conflicts.

4. Then completely uninstall & re-install Office and see the results.

If you need further help, to make sure you receive expert help, it is suggested that you post the thread with the confirmed information above in the Office 2016 for Mac forum, which is a specialized support channel for dealing with the Office 2016 for Mac usability related issues, such as PowerPoint 2016 for mac crashing. We appreciate your understanding.

Best Regards,
Jim

Hi,

I am looking at doing cutover migration. We are using Exchange Hosted services from 3rd party email service provider. Hosted Exchange is Exchange 2010 SP3. Now we have decided to move email services to Office 365. In office 365, we have already provisioned user account in office 365 from On premise Active Directory using AADconnect. Exchange online licenses are not assigned to users. Microsoft BI and Visio are being used by users in office 365.

In one of the post, I read that if Exchange and Lync Online licenses are not assigned to users, then cutover method can be used to migrate mailboxes to Exchange Online, considering I disable the AADConnect sync. I wanted confirmation if cutover is feasible in this scenario. In this scenario, user account is being synced from ON Premise Active Directory whereas mailbox is being migrated from 3rd party service provider.

if yes, then how distribution group and shared mailboxes will be migrated.

Regards

Rajkumar

a. user say:

Hi Rajkumar,

If the user accounts have already been synced from on-premises server to Office 365, the scenario is not supported by Microsoft and not feasible either, although Exchange and Skype for Business licenses are not assigned to users.

Thanks for your understanding,
Edward

rajkumar d chaurasia say:

Thanks Edward,

My query is resolved.

Regards

rajkumar

ganesh achar b say:

Hi,

 

Refer to these methods and check.

 

Method 1:

Modern User Internet Explorer 11 doesn't allow saving pages in the usual way. You can however save the page as PDF if you have Microsoft OneNote installed.

a. Bring up the Devices charm using Windows + K Keys together

b. Finally choose Send To One Note to save the page in PDF format

c. If you have a printer attached it'll show up in the Devices charm. Select it to print the webpage.

 

Method 2:

Set the Reader program as the default program and try and save and print. Refer to the following links.

Set program access and computer defaults.

Excel hours and minutes to decimal vlue query - Microsoft Community

markmcmc say:

Excel hours and minutes to decimal vlue query

I've just joined a company that gets a couple hundred overtime returns in in Excel and in the format of

1.15 or 1.25 or 1.45

where 1.15 is 1 hour 15 minutes

What is the quickest way to convert this number into a decimal value of 1.25. 

Mark

 

ashish mathur say:

Hi,

Try this

=DOLLARDE(A2,60)

Hope this helps.

hansv mvp say:

Let's say you have a "time" such as 1.15 in A1.

The following formula will convert it to decimal hours:

=INT(A1)+100*MOD(A1,1)/60

Excel 2010 not copying hidden columns - Microsoft Community

dmoser22 say:

Excel 2010 not copying hidden columns

I've found loads of posts online explaining how to copy only unhidden cells, but none on what to do when I want to copy hidden cells.  This was working perfectly until I "upgraded" to Windows 10.  Since upgrading to Windows 10, when I select a whole row that contains hidden columns and copy it, it is only grabbing the visible columns.  According to Excel help, this is supposed to be the default behavior, but it isn't working for me.  How can I get it to go back to copy all columns, including the hidden ones?

dmoser22 say:

Thanks for your response.

I opened Excel in Safe Mode as you described, and it still did not work properly.

After that, I tried recreating the issue in a blank workbook, but could not.

I was able to resolve the issue using these steps:

  • I opened the workbook having the problem, plus a new empty workbook.
  • In the original workbook, I unhid all columns in all worksheets, then copied the contents of each sheet to a corresponding sheet in the new workbook.
  • In the new workbook, I hid the appropriate columns again, tested it out, and everything works.

All I can figure was that something was corrupted in the original that was fixed by copying the data into a new sheet.  I don't know if it was related in any way to the Windows 10 upgrade; I simply noticed that the problem first occurred at that time.

Anyway - thanks for your help!

-djm

monkey57 say:

Look in your 'Programs and Features' for anything Yahoo, remove it, then change your default search engine in each browser...

Please consider reviewing the following, and running the bleepingcomputer tools, and malwarebytes:

For the protection of what is important (if win8/10):

Make sure your FileHistory backup is up-to-date (right click start, control panel, FileHistory-Turn it On). (it requires a usb external harddrive (Windows 8/10 will, automatically, create the FileHistory folder on the usb drive, when FileHistory is turned On);  or network harddrive can be used (make a 'FileHistory' folder on the Network Harddrive to connect the app to).... If you keep things in non-standard places, make new Libraries, and add the folders to your custom Libraries. Check to see where quicken , printer scan-to folders, or any other user installed software is saving data.  (You can backup quicken/intuit programs to a OneDrive folder, but do not let database files reside in OneDrive;  although, they can be included in Libraries (and probably already are), they will not backup when open.  (some (other) databases can not be restored easily from raw data alone).

see:

http://windows.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/libraries-faq#1TC=windows-8

If you suspect malicious activity or malware (in any version of windows);  use these tools from bleepingcomputer (they are relatively quick):  http://www.bleepingcomputer.com/download/adwcleaner/ (the other two (2) suggested tools are on the bottom of that page), like rkill (1), jrt [junkware removal tool] (2), and adwcleaner (3) (run all of them, in that sequence)(i put them on the desktop, and run them from there)(as administrator (right click))(if they get hung (10 min) for any reason, close the running tool, go to the next tool, after trying them all, if any are unsuccessful, re-run them again (in sequence) in safe mode;  also run Malwarebytes, while in safe mode during this process (if its definitions are updated), before adwcleaner.  Uninstall adwcleaner, after running it and the system has rebooted, by opening the program, and choosing the uninstall button, or its quarantined files may set off your antivirus. The other tools from bleepingcomputer can be safely deleted, after running them; they are updated often, so the old versions are not necessary. After running the tools, if they found anything, you need to reset all your browsers to default, then check for any unfamiliar plugin/addins within the browser. then run malwarebytes  again.

in a lot of instances,  you have to remove the malicious activity one layer at a time, so you may not want to delete the tools after the first run.

Run Malwarebytes (Free):

https://www.malwarebytes.org/mwb-download/

uncheck the box at the end of the install for trial, or convert to free at the end of the trial.

Malwarebyes is a good addition to your antivirus software. Make sure in Malwarebytes the 'Scan for rootkits' box is checked-> Settings-Detection and Protection.  Free means manual, so, you have to open it, and run it occasionally.

geek uninstaller can help to uninstall programs that are unusual, it works on 32-bit and x64 programs (and it stays free)

http://www.geekuninstaller.com/download

only get the free version.

right click on the program in geek, will let you force uninstall, without running the apps native uninstaller (only use the force method, if the installed program is malicious, or will not uninstall normally). 

Try HerdProtect (free),  http://www.herdprotect.com/  ,be watchful of false positives, only remove unchecked items at the end (by putting a check in the box), if they reside in a temp type folder or you are sure about them, remember to run it again in a few hrs(per mfg instructions).  I, generally, recommend uninstalling HerdProtect,  after a few weeks, as it's cache gets large fast.

***Pre-installed or user previously installed antivirus may inhibit the current antivirus (even a current norton installation), use the mfg removal tools to completely remove them, if they were ever on your system.***

Use the mfg removal tools to completely remove them, after running the uninstall in Programs and features see:

https://service.mcafee.com/FAQDocument.aspx?id=TS101331

(MCPR is 1/2 way down the page)

or

Norton Removal tool at:

https://support.norton.com/sp/en/us/home/current/solutions/kb20080710133834EN_EndUserProfile_en_us

For AVG removal see:

http://www.avg.com/us-en/utilities

in addition to the removal tool for your version of AVG.

Use the 'AVG Identity Protection Remover'

List of anti-malware product removal tools

http://answers.microsoft.com/en-us/protect/wiki/mse-protect_start/list-of-anti-malware-product-removal-tools/2bcb53f7-7ab4-4ef9-ab3a-6aebfa322f75

After, you have run the bleepingcomputer tools(etc) mentioned earlier;

Run System File Checker

Click on Start > Type CMD

Right click on CMD > Select Run As Administrator

Type sfc /scannow  Note:  there is a space between sfc and /scannow

Press Enter to start the scan

For stray startup entries.  Try autoruns:

https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/sysinternals/bb963902

You can uncheck entries, to disable them.  And you can delete them, afterwards, if you determine it boots normal.

Expand the window, and stretch columns, so you can see all of path.  DO NOT DELETE "File not found" entries, unless you are absolutely sure of them.

Please read the manual.  

Check your browser desktop/taskbar shortcuts, remove them and re-add to taskbar/desktop.

Manually check for Windows Updates.

If you have a desired 3rd party(non-Microsoft) product, please refer to their support to resolve compatibility issues in win8/10, or other versions of Microsoft Windows.

IFERROR and AVERAGEIF on early versions of Office - Microsoft Community

bubba070 say:

IFERROR and AVERAGEIF on early versions of Office

How do I get =IFERROR(AVERAGEIF(C5:C5000,"F",D5:D5000),"") to work in early versions of excel? It works on my Excel 2010 but does not work on my work computers that have Excel 2000. I dont think either IFERROR or AVERAGEIF work prior to 2007. What could I use?

Thanks


jaeson cardaño say:
How do I get =IFERROR(AVERAGEIF(C5:C5000,"F",D5:D5000),"") to work in early versions of excel? It works on my Excel 2010 but does not work on my work computers that have Excel 2000. I dont think either IFERROR or AVERAGEIF work prior to 2007. What could I use?


Hi bubba,

 

Try this...

 

=IF(ISERROR(SUMIF(C5:C500,"F",D5:D500)/COUNTIF(C5:C500,"F")),"",SUMIF(C5:C500,"F",D5:D500)/COUNTIF(C5:C500,"F"))

 

Hope it helps,

Jaeson

v_agarwal say:

Replace with

=IF(ISERROR(SUMPRODUCT(--(C5:C5000="F"),D5:D5000)/COUNTIF(C5:C5000,"F")),0,SUMPRODUCT(--(C5:C5000="F"),D5:D5000)/COUNTIF(C5:C5000,"F"))

Changing Skype Username - Microsoft Community

scubadivermag say:

Changing Skype Username

I'm using Skype desktop and when signing up it forces a stupidly long username on me. How do I go about changing this to something that is more memorable and personal to me?

I want ScubaDiverMag which would relate to me but can find any way of changing it so people can find me this way.

***Skype name was masked for security and privacy purposes.

aljon_t say:

Hi

After the migration of all Skype accounts to Microsoft account, newly created Skype account will have a system-generated Skype name with the prefix "live:" in it. Furthermore, please be guided the Skype name is not possible to change or modify as it is a unique identifier of every Skype account. On the contrary, what you can change to your preferred name is your Skype display name.

You may refer to this link for additional information: How do I change my Skype display name?

Hope this information helps. Feel free to post back if you have questions and clarifications.

Regards.

Using Onenote as Journal - Microsoft Community

troybom say:

Using Onenote as Journal

I want to start using Onenote as a journal.  I titled the notebook "journal."  Then I titled the sections as the months.  My question is:

Is there a way when I add a new page for that page to automatically be titled as the current date?  I know that the date is stamped on it, but then I still have to change "untitled" to the date.

Thanks in advance, for any help.

jr de pijper say:
               
Is there a way when I add a new page for that page to automatically be titled as the current date?  I know that the date is stamped on it, but then I still have to change "untitled" to the date.

No, there isn't. What I usually do is go to the latest entry, then select the title (ctrl-shift-T), copy (ctrl-C), create a new page (ctrl-N), paste the title (ctrl-V) and then change the title to the new day.

petrib say: There's no built-in voicemail in the phone. It is a network service, so ask your network operator (or "carrier", if you're in the USA), if they didn't provide you instructions already.
